## Strategy in brief
EMA5/8/13 + RSI + ADX scalper on 5m, BTC-macro-gated. Entry passes a BTC/pair filter stack вҶ’ sized by liquidity caps Г— multiplier/pattern-cell rules вҶ’ exited by a tiered ladder.

### Exit stack (current)
- **FAST_EXIT OFF** (both L1 +0.20%/2min and L2 disabled).
- **ATR-LOW Fixed TP (LONG) вҖ” DISABLED 2026-06-09** (`atr_low_fixed_tp_long_enabled=false`). Paired with "Keep Only Unmatched Longs" (below): the fix-TP caps the pop-and-fade (matched) cohort, but the unmatched longs we now keep are RUNNERS (54% peak вүҘ0.40) вҖ” capping them at +0.25 strangled the edge. OFF so unmatched longs trail. **Coupling: re-enable the fix-TP if `long_unmatched_only` is ever turned OFF (matched longs need the cap).**
- **рҹ§¬ KEEP ONLY UNMATCHED LONGS вҖ” SHIPPED 2026-06-09 (in-sample, forward-test)** (`long_unmatched_only=true`). Blocks any LONG matching ANY C or W pattern (counter `LONG_UNMATCHED_ONLY`); keep only truly-unmatched longs. **Evidence (10-pool, current-stack: fix-TP + EMA13-off + wide-SL + multipliers):** the LONG pattern library uniformly selects for LOSERS вҖ” EVERY C/W pattern net-negative (W6 вҲ’$574, W2 вҲ’$480, C7 вҲ’$261, C6 вҲ’$297 demux; multiplier *amplifies* the matched losses); truly-unmatched longs = N=39, **85% WR, +$471 demux / +$679 as-sized** (the UNMATCHED-LONG 2Г— sits correctly on them). Keep-only-unmatched flips the long book **вҲ’$1,515 вҶ’ +$471 demux** (blocks ~80% of longs). With fix-TP off + trailing, the unmatched cohort models +$1,500вҖ“3,200 (heavy haircut on the trailing model). Mechanism: matched-long patterns = countertrend/exhaustion signatures (C7 bounce, W6 top); no-pattern = clean momentum runner. **FORWARD-TEST READ GATE: does the unmatched-long cohort hold вүҘ70% WR AND net-positive demux on NвүҘ20 fresh full-stack? If yes вҶ’ keep. If unmatched WR<60% OR net-negative on NвүҘ20 вҶ’ revert (toggle off + re-enable fix-TP).** In-sample + N=39 вҶ’ forward-validate before calling it proven. SHORT side already mirror-optimal (truly-unmatched shorts blocked; matched shorts carry the edge).
- **Trailing**: arms at peak вүҘ **0.45%** (tp_min), exits at peak вҲ’ **0.25%** (pullback, ATR-floored Г—0.5 + 0.1/level widen).
- **Trailing Min-Profit Gate (shipped 2026-06-08): `trailing_min_profit_to_fire = +0.10`.** The price-drop trailing only fires when its exit level (peak вҲ’ pullback) is вүҘ +0.10%; below that it's **suppressed/dormant** (rides the hard SL, re-arms on recovery). Fixes high-ATR L1 whipsaws where the ATR-widened pullback exceeds the peak (peak +0.45 вҲ’ pullback 0.67 = вҲ’0.22 вҶ’ exits red on a pair that recovers). Self-scopes to L1 (L2+ always clears). Engine: `indicators.py` price-drop fire gated on `(peak_pnl вҲ’ pullback) вүҘ +0.10`.
- **Runner Stretch-Trail** (LONG, high-ATR) **OFF (disabled 2026-06-06, `runner_trail_enabled`=false)** вҖ” high-ATR runners now exit via normal tight trailing. Live RUNNER_TRAIL exits were a wash (N=6, net +$30 vs tight, 3/6 better, and the bigger peakers FADED вҖ” stretch-trail gave back more than tight). UI toggle added (flip back on anytime). (The high-ATR ATR Multiplier sizing dimension that lived alongside this was REMOVED Jun 10 вҖ” see Active multipliers section.)
- **EMA13 strict cross exit вҖ” SHORT closes; LONG in PHANTOM-CF mode (Jun 7).** `ema13_cross_exit_long_enabled=false`: the cross no longer closes LONGs вҖ” it records a phantom (would-have-exited pnl, `phantom_ema13_cross_pnl`) and the long rides to its real exit. Tracked in the **рҹ”Җ EMA13 Cross вҖ” Disabled-Direction CF** table. SHORT still closes normally.
- **SL: signal-DEAD (STOP_LOSS) = вҲ’0.70% base; signal-ACTIVE (STOP_LOSS_WIDE) = вҲ’1.00% base (`signal_active_sl`, widened 2026-06-06 from вҲ’0.70).** Both ATR-widened (Г—1.5, floor вҲ’1.20%). The two labels differ only by whether the entry signal was still valid at the stop вҖ” now the signal-active path gets +0.30% more room (thesis still alive вҶ’ ride; thesis dead вҶ’ exit tight). VERY_STRONG + STRONG_BUY only.
- **Pattern fixed exits**: C1 SHORT fixed_sl вҲ’0.70%.
- **BE is OFF** (be_levels_enabled false). RSI-handoff OFF. Regime-change-exit OFF.

## рҹ“Ӣ GO-LIVE TODO (future вҖ” not urgent in paper; build before/at live scale-up)
- **в‘  BalanceвҶ’leverage schedule (de-lever-as-you-grow risk knob; sibling of liquidity sizing) вҖ” 2026-06-26.** New config field `leverage_balance_schedule = "0:20, 10000:15, 25000:10, 100000:5"` (balance_usd : max_lev tiers; empty = OFF = current 20Г—). Engine: one clamp where leverage is set вҖ” `sched_cap = _lookup_schedule(schedule, current_equity)` then `leverage = min(confidence_lev, sched_cap)`; sits alongside the existing hard-cap clamp, composes with cell `lev_mult`, fully deterministic (steps down automatically as balance crosses thresholds, no manual call). Observability: header readout ("lev cap: 15Г— @ $12k", like the GROSS gauge). **вҡ  The tier VALUES above are round GUESSES вҖ” the whole point is that they should be DATA-DRIVEN from the tail-stressed blended-pool Kelly (see below), not placeholders.** Genuinely INERT at $3.7k (tier 0:20 вҶ’ min(20,20)=20Г— = no change), so safe to ship off/empty. RATIONALE: compounding punishes variance quadratically (gвүҲОјвҲ’ПғВІ/2; leverage scales ОјвҲқL but ПғВІвҲқLВІ) вҶ’ a +EV strategy at too-high leverage has NEGATIVE compound growth; fat gap-tail + correlated-dump pulls growth-optimal leverage below 20Г—; as stakes get real, shift growth-max вҶ’ ruin-aversion (fractional Kelly). Ties to scaling roadmap (ruin risk = binding constraint).
  - **рҹ“җ v3 OPERATING PLAN (2026-07-02, operator-ratified вҖ” SUPERSEDES the 07-01 11-tier G/L design AND the guess tiers): working-capital reserve = PRIMARY (вң… BUILT 2026-07-02), coarse 4-tier lev schedule = backstop.** Architecture: slippage/capacity = per-pair 0.1% cap + $500k ceiling (adaptive, the TRUE capacity governor вҖ” a global gross target was the wrong tool, operator-corrected); ruin = `reserve_mode="working_capital"` + `working_capital_target` (tradeable = min(available, target), reserve auto-grows, withdrawals pull FROM the reserve; engine at the safe-reserve calc, UI = Reserve Mode dropdown 3rd option, D11 full; **superseded same day by the AUTO SCHEDULE вҖ” operator: "all automatic, not me putting 40000 manually"**: `reserve_mode="schedule"` + `reserve_schedule="10000:8000, 25000:17500, 50000:27500, 100000:40000, 150000:50000, 250000:70000, 500000:100000"` вҖ” вң… SHIPPED **ON** (engine walks the v3 table itself via the same tier-lookup as the lev schedule; below $10k вҶ’ no reserve = full balance, so inert today; between milestones the reserve absorbs ALL growth; withdrawals pull from the reserve and it self-rebuilds automatically вҖ” no config action ever needed). UI: 4th Reserve-Mode option + a BalanceвҶ’Tradeable row-editor table (mirrors the lev-schedule editor, live readout) + balance-card Reserve line turns emerald when active; violence backstop = lev schedule **4 tiers only: `0:20, 25000:15, 75000:10, 250000:5` вҖ” вң… SET IN CONFIG 2026-07-02** (`leverage_balance_schedule`, inert at $3k). **Max gross leverage 30Г—вҶ’25Г— SHIPPED** (binds only vs multiplier stacks = the correlated-dump moment; per-position lev stays 20Г—, the cap is ОЈnotional and blocks the NEXT entry). **v3 milestone schedule (operator-set, more aggressive than v2; anchor = $150kвҶ’save $100k/trade $50k):** $10kвҶ’reserve 20% В· $25kвҶ’30% В· $50kвҶ’45% В· $100kвҶ’60% ($40k trade) В· **$150kвҶ’67% ($100k reserved / $50k trade)** В· $250kвҶ’72% ($70k trade) В· $500kвҶ’80% (**$100k trade = the working capacity-ceiling hypothesis, validated/moved by `exit_slippage_pct` telemetry**) В· beyondвҶ’hold trade вүҲ$100k, reserve absorbs all growth. Worst correlated-cluster loss falls 24%вҶ’~1% of balance along the path; with isolated margin the absolute worst case (all-5 liquidated, liq вүҲ вҲ’4.7% price at 20Г— vs SL вҲ’0.7..вҲ’1.2 = ~4Г— buffer; residual = gap/outage вҶ’ the в‘Ў server-side stop item) = the WORKING CAPITAL only, reserve untouchable. At each milestone: flip `working_capital_target` to the table value (mode working_capital) вҖ” one manual action, keeps the operator in the de-risk loop.
  - **вң… RESOLVED 2026-06-29 вҖ” ATR-SPECIFIC vol-scaling is REFUTED; the de-lever lever is GLOBAL only (this schedule), NOT per-pair sizing. CLOSES the "high-ATR tail" thread вҖ” do NOT re-litigate.** Tested constant-$-risk sizing (size вҲқ 1/effective-SL, so the ATR-widened вҲ’1.20 pairs shrink to 0.58Г— to match a вҲ’0.70 trade's $ risk) on the screened pool: **total $ +$3001 вҶ’ +$2240 = вҲ’$761 (вҲ’25%)** for only вҲ’21% per-trade Пғ вҖ” and the rough geometric check shows the вҲ’25% mean hit DWARFS the ПғВІ/2 benefit, so it lowers compound growth too. Why: high-ATR is **net-POSITIVE** ($ by band: 0.47-0.80 = +$1628, вүҘ0.80 = +$1249; вүҘ0.80 wins +$1960 vs loses вҲ’$711) вҶ’ vol-scaling de-sizes the WINNERS more than the losers (PUMP/SUI +1.0-1.9% runners > the вҲ’1.20 losers). **The вҲ’1.20 high-ATR losses (SKYAI/MANTA/AGLD) are NOT a gap-through вҖ” they hit the engine's ATR-WIDENED вҲ’1.20 stop by design (`sl_atr_multiplier=1.5` capped at `sl_atr_widen_floor_pct=вҲ’1.20`), the RIGHT exit for the net-positive high-ATR runners.** They are the irreducible left-tail cost of a +EV cohort (same wall as flip-shorts / unmatched-long cell вҖ” winners & losers feature-inseparable). EVERY angle now refuted: entry-filter (high-ATR wins), exit (fast-exit вҲ’$195 post-filter), cell-cut (inseparable), ATR-sizing (вҲ’$761). **The ONLY lever is GLOBAL de-lever = pure risk-appetite (ruin-aversion), NOT an optimization** вҖ” it sacrifices ~25%+ return for lower drawdown; pull it only if balance gets thin / ruin becomes the binding constraint. At a healthy balance the вҲ’1.20 losses are variance to tolerate.
  - **PREREQ (data, do FIRST): tail-stressed blended-pool Kelly.** Build a BLENDED long+short pool (full trade set across the curated batches, NOT flip-shorts only) and run `maximize g(e)=E[ln(1+eВ·m_i)]` with losers' fills stressed to their in-trade/post-exit troughs (paper truncates the tail at the clean SL вҶ’ biases Kelly HIGH). Output = growth-optimal exposure вҶ’ de-lever tiers. **Note 2026-06-26:** ran it on the FLIP-SHORT-ONLY 5-batch pool (N=104) вҶ’ e*=**0Г—** in all 3 tail scenarios because that sleeve's mean is NEGATIVE (вҲ’0.014%/trade realized, вҲ’0.636% gap-stressed, worst вҲ’10.17%) вҶ’ Kelly won't lever a zero-edge coin flip AT ALL. That's a verdict on the SLEEVE (de-lever the flip-short sleeve toward observation), not the account. The account number needs the LONG sleeve blended in (longs are the edge: today's batch +$960/+0.58%/trade). Expected blended answer вүҲ 8вҖ“14Г— (below current 20Г—).
  - **рҹ“җ CAPITAL-SCALING STRATEGY (operator-chosen 2026-06-30 вҖ” DESIGN registered, BUILD DEFERRED until forward-validated & balance approaches the first tier; no-op at $3k).** Goal = **$1M *banked* (withdrawn), NOT $1M in-account** вҶ’ less ruin exposure. Three composed knobs, with the primary being the RESERVE (not the leverage curve):
>     1. **Reserve as the PRIMARY de-risk knob, reframed as "fixed working capital".** Today `reserve` is static (`reserve_percentage=20`; engine line ~2124 `tradeable = balance вҲ’ reserve`). Build a `reserve_mode="working_capital"` + `working_capital_target` ($, 0=off): `tradeable = min(available вҲ’ floor, target)`, so the reserve % **auto-grows** with balance to keep deployed capital вүҲ constant. WHY this over the leverage curve: our real tail is **5 CORRELATED positions stopping together** вҖ” reserve caps *total deployed* regardless of correlation (the leverage curve only shrinks each of the 5, still deploys all). Property: **max correlated-cluster loss stays clamped at a fixed $** (вүҲ working_capital Г— SL% Г— lev) no matter how big the account gets вҶ’ true ruin bound. e.g. $50k working cap вҶ’ ~$7-10k max cluster loss whether the account is $60k or $500k.
>     2. **вҮ’ The balanceвҶ’leverage schedule (в‘  above) then goes FLAT, not descending.** `exposure вүҲ (1вҲ’reserve%)Г—lev` вҖ” with reserve fixing working capital, a *descending* lev curve would DOUBLE de-risk (kills compounding). So with working-capital mode ON: leverage stays **constant** on the working capital (and the в‘  schedule must be re-keyed to working-capital or disabled, else it reads TOTAL balance and de-levers twice). Pick ONE primary: **reserve-primary + flat lev** (recommended, better for the correlated tail) OR the в‘  descending-lev curve with reserve 0 вҖ” not both aggressive.
>     3. **Periodic REAL withdrawals still required.** Reserve protects vs *trading* losses but stays ON the exchange (platform/hack risk) and doesn't *realize* the $1M. Operator's skim plan (withdraw $100k per +$150k gained) is the realize step вҖ” but **calibrate the early phase**: a FIXED $150k threshold makes cycle-1 from a small base require a huge % run (+1500% from $10k) with nothing banked = max ruin exposure exactly when most fragile. FIX: **(a) return the initial stake ASAP** (once ~2-3Г—, pull the original capital вҶ’ zero personal-ruin risk from day 1); **(b) skim proportionally early** (% of each gain), switching to the fixed $100k/$150k cadence only once the account is ~$100k+ where $150k is a sane %.
>     - **CALIBRATION (do FIRST, with data): the working_capital size is set from the forward MAX-DRAWDOWN + the correlation of the 5 concurrent positions (NвүҘ30 forward), NOT guessed.** Ties to the tail-stressed Kelly prereq (line ~77). Build only when balance nears the first tier.
>     4. **рҹ“Ҹ CAPACITY CEILING is the second calibration input (operator-ratified 2026-07-01 вҖ” "de-lever vs fixed $50k volume" resolved: SEQUENCED, fixed cap is the ENDGAME).** The strategy has a market-dictated max size: the edge (+0.2-0.4%/trade net) scalps thin alts and is fragile to slippage, which grows with order size вҖ” somewhere ~$10-30k/position marginal slippage eats the marginal edge, and no capital fixes that. So: de-lever/ramp = the transition; **fixed working capital (вүҲ fixed max tradable volume) = the destination** вҖ” it aligns with the real constraint, makes drawdown-% shrink automatically as balance grows (ruinвҶ’0), and is one revisable number vs a schedule to mis-tune. **Do NOT pick the cap a priori ($50k is a placeholder): measure it from `exit_slippage_pct` telemetry as size scales (slippage-vs-notional curve; cap where marginal slippage eats вүҘ~30% of the per-trade edge).** The binding calibration wins: min(risk-based cap from DD+correlation [pt 3], capacity cap from slippage). Linear in-account growth at the ceiling is FINE вҖ” wealth realizes via the withdrawal plan (pt 3), not in-account compounding. Want more than the ceiling? вҶ’ a SECOND strategy (the parked BTC 4h Donchian module), never more size on this one.
- **в‘Ў Server-side reduce-only stop-market backstop (closes the bot-outage gap-tail hole) вҖ” 2026-06-26.** Live SL is currently a SOFTWARE/monitored stop (bot watches WS price вҶ’ fires market order w/ 3Г— bounded retry); NO resting exchange-side stop вҶ’ a bot/WS outage or violent gap has no server-side safety net (the `protective_sl_order_id` column is vestigial/unwired). FIX: place a reduce-only STOP_MARKET on Binance at open so the exchange closes near the level even if the bot dies. **вҡ  HISTORY: attempted before and REMOVED вҖ” it generated Binance errors on close trades** (likely reduce-only/qty/precision conflict with the bot's own market close racing the resting stop). So a re-attempt MUST solve the dual-close race (e.g. cancel the resting stop in the close path before the bot's own market close, or make the resting stop the SOLE close mechanism for SL exits). Not a paper concern (paper fills the SL clean at trigger, ~0 slippage); strictly a live-hardening item. The everyday live fill is ~SL+slippage (вүҲвҲ’1 to вҲ’1.5%), NOT the вҲ’4.77% worst-case trough; the resting stop closes the rare violent-gap/outage tail.

### рҹ—“ 2026-06-21 watchlist (observation вҖ” no ship)

GOAL: decide whether to flip `regime_change_exit` ON for a specific cohort = bail when BTC regime turns mid-trade instead of riding to SL. вҡ пёҸ **CRITICAL CAVEAT (diagnosed 2026-06-22 вҖ” the table is NOT what it looks like):** it fires on the **3-value MACRO regime** (`determine_macro_regime`, EMA20-slope BULLISH/NEUTRAL/BEARISH) going NEUTRAL/opposite mid-trade вҖ” which is a DIFFERENT system than the FINE regime (STRONG_BULLвҶ’BULL_EXHAUSTEDвҶ’CHOPPY) every other table uses. Consequences: (a) it's **structurally LONG-biased** вҖ” counter-trend shorts (PAIR_RSI_OB, adverse macro AT ENTRY) can never produce a favorableвҶ’neutralвҶ’opposite sequence, so they show **0 rows** even though they drifted in fine-regime terms (19 shorts drifted, 0 stamped); (b) `regime_neutral_pnl`/`regime_opposite_pnl` only populate for trades that lived through a macro-NEUTRAL window mid-trade. So the counterfactual currently answers "should LONGS bail when the macro TREND flips" вҖ” NOT a general loser-cut. For the analysis: split OPPOSITE(adverse) vs NEUTRAL(soft) вҖ” adverse mostly dies (exit wins), soft recovers ~в…“ (exiting chops comebacks); a positive О” (holdвҲ’exit) means exiting earlier WOULD have helped. If the longs-only cut is strong, consider either shipping `regime_change_exit` long-only OR re-basing the trigger on the FINE regime to capture the shorts too (bigger change вҖ” flag before building). All pure read-only views (no engine/config). Early reads to date are on the MIXED pre-reset pool (N=278, scaffolding only) вҖ” judge on the fresh single-config data. Supersedes/consolidates the 06-20 'ATR-THEORY TABLES' build note.

Mechanism: fading into an exhausting bear = the bounce runs the short over. в‘ў **WINNER CELL (multiplier track): qsвүҘ3 AND bear%вүҘ70 AND range 60-90** вҖ” in-sample N=14/~79%WR/+0.49%/+$671. **вҡ  в‘ &в‘Ў OVERLAP HEAVILY вҖ” they are largely the SAME loser slice (low-range fade in an exhausted bear):** of the N=72 cohort, range<50 вҲ© BEAR_EXHAUSTED = 4 trades; UNION (range<50 OR BEX) = only 10 unique (8+6вҲ’4). range<50 captures 4 of the 6 BEX losers; BEX adds only ~$114 unique on top. **Block-impact on N=72 (baseline 61.1%WR/+0.038%/+$147.5):** block range<50 вҶ’ 64t/64.1%/+0.099%/+$536 (О”+$388) В· block BEX вҶ’ 66t/63.6%/+0.081%/+$455 (О”+$307) В· block UNION вҶ’ 62t/64.5%/+0.120%/+$650 (О”+$502, NOT +$695 вҖ” overlap, don't double-count). **вҮ’ TREAT range<50 AS THE PRIMARY (broader, mechanism-fundamental) filter; BEX is the small non-overlapping residual.** Concentrate the forward-N accrual on range<50. **Confound test (the key result): QS and the dimensions are INDEPENDENT** вҖ” within the favorable (bearвүҘ70 & range60-90) bucket, qs=2 still loses (N=12/42%/вҲ’0.110%) while qsвүҘ3 wins (+0.43..+0.55%); so they STACK (block dial = dimensions; floor dial = qs; multiply dial = qsвүҘ3Г—good-dims). **Dimensions are SHARPER block candidates than qs=2** (which is 51%WR/вҲ’0.07% diffuse, fails the C-gate, and contains winners вҖ” see line above). qs=2-specific carve REJECTED: within qs=2, breadth is a non-monotonic confound, W-vs-L entry means are near-identical (feature-inseparable), loss diffuse across 23 pairs. **PROMOTE (primary path): range<50 FLIP-SHORT block вҶ’ ship only at NвүҘ30 FORWARD holding WRвүӨ40% AND avgвүӨвҲ’0.20% (C-gate); re-check whether BEX adds unique value beyond range<50 before adding it separately. Winner cell вҶ’ multiplier track per the qsвүҘ3 line's gate.** No config/code change. вҶ’ DECISION_LOG 2026-06-26.

- **рҹ“Ҡ ATR-THEORY TABLES вҖ” BUILT 2026-06-21 (3 tables; ANALYZE on the fresh batch).** Surfaces under 'Performance by Pair ATR(14)%': в‘  ATR Г— Hold-Time cross-tab (commit 80c4a20) В· в‘Ў **вҸұ Hold-Time Г— ATR** (duration-primary, the EFFECT side: WR / RegChg% / avg-ATR by duration band) В· в‘ў **рҹҺІ Regime-Drift Г— Outcome** (HELD entry==exit vs DRIFTED entryвү exit, Г— direction вҖ” the decisive "driftвҶ’random" test). EARLY READ on the mixed pre-reset pool (N=278, **scaffolding only**): avg-ATR falls monotonically with hold (1.13%вҶ’0.24%) & RegChg% climbs (26%вҶ’100%), BUT WR does NOT cleanly decay; **drift HURTS longs (HELD 55% vs DRIFTED 40%/вҲ’0.25%) but does NOT hurt fade-shorts (HELD 51% vs DRIFTED 53%/вҲ’0.00%)** вҖ” a fade WANTS the reversal, which IS a regime change вҶ’ the "driftвҶ’random" thesis is **LONG-only**. Confirm on clean single-config data. в”Җв”Җв”Җ orig theory + validation: THEORY (operator): high ATR = fast-resolving trades (hit the fixed Вұ% stops quickly, while the entry thesis still holds); low ATR = slow trades where BTC conditions drift from entry вҶ’ random outcome. VALIDATED on pooled N=278: **ATRвҶ’speed CONFIRMED monotonic** (median hold: <0.5% ATR = 28m вҶ’ 0.5-1 = 11m вҶ’ 1-1.5 = 6m вҶ’ 1.5-2.5 = 4m вҶ’ >2.5 = 2m); **regime-drift CONFIRMED monotonic by hold-time** (entryвү exit BTC regime: <10m = 26% вҶ’ 10-20 = 45% вҶ’ 20-40 = 67% вҶ’ 40-90 = 74% вҶ’ **>90m = 100%**); lowest-ATR <0.5 = 50%WR/вҲ’0.09 coin flip w/ 63% drift. **CAVEATS: (a) WR does NOT cleanly decay with hold (zig-zags 48вҶ’60вҶ’45вҶ’59вҶ’42%) вҖ” randomness shows at the EXTREMES, not monotonically; (b) STRATEGY CONFOUND вҖ” high-ATR вүҲ FAN shorts (runner edge), low-ATR вүҲ bull-longs/momentum вҶ’ SPLIT BY DIRECTION is mandatory or it reads as an ATR edge that's really a sleeve edge.** BUILD: `_compute_atr_holdtime_crosstab(orders)` in main.py; rows = ATR bands (<0.5/0.5-1/1-1.5/1.5-2.5/>2.5) Г— dur cols (<10/10-20/20-40/40-90/>90m), cell = N/WR%/avg%, LONG & SHORT split in-table, marginals per ATR row = median-hold + regime-change%; placed under 'Performance by Pair ATR(14)%'. - **рҹҸғ BE-RATCHET + N=0.5вҶ’1.0 вҖ” SHIPPED 2026-06-17 (operator).** *[N PORTION SUPERSEDED 2026-06-17 PM вҖ” N reverted/held at 0.5 and the give-back cap was first added then DISABLED; see the give-back-DISABLED entry above for current state. BE-ratchet (lock) is unchanged and still LIVE.]* Fixes "peaked +0.5% then closed negative." ROOT CAUSE (mechanism, not noise): on high-ATR/modest-peak shorts the give-back `NГ—ATR` EXCEEDS the peak, so the chandelier floor `peak вҲ’ NГ—ATR` sits BELOW breakeven вҶ’ permits a full round-trip into a loss or to the вҲ’0.70 SL. Discriminator is **peak/ATR, NOT ATR level** вҖ” the 2 highest-ATR trades (ESPORTS 2.63, BR 2.01) were fine because they peaked >1.7; the 5 broken ones (EVAA ATR1.89/pk0.59вҶ’вҲ’0.36, VELVET ATR1.59/pk0.76вҶ’вҲ’1.20, PORTALГ—2, AERO) all peaked +0.49вҖ“0.76. **FIX = BE-ratchet:** once armed, exit floor = `max(peak вҲ’ NГ—ATR, be_lock_pct)`, `be_lock=0.10` (вүҲnet-flat after 0.09% fee). Only binds when `peak вҲ’ NГ—ATR < lock` (the broken set) вҶ’ by construction CANNOT touch a runner (PORTAL floor 1.96 unchanged). Config `runner_trail_short_be_ratchet_enabled`=true + `runner_trail_short_be_lock_pct`=0.10; live in the realtime flip-strpk block (fire when `pnl_pct <= eff_floor`, reason tags lock vs atr). **PAIRED: `runner_trail_short_atr_mult` 0.5вҶ’1.0** вҖ” the ratchet caps the reverser tail, so the looser N is now safe and gives genuine runners room (sim 23 armed: N=1.0+ratchet +20.05% vs N=0.5 +14.02%; вҡ пёҸ +4.5 of the +5 edge is ONE trade, PORTAL 2.70вҶ’7.20, + post-exit-continuation inflation вҖ” runner-dependent, NOT +5%/day expectation; N=1.0 also costs ~0.1вҖ“0.15%/trade on the low-ATR book). Both changes act on DISJOINT sets (ratchetвҶ’reversers, NвҶ’runners) so attribution stays clean. **`shadow_atr05` (N=0.5, no-ratchet) is the control.** **REVERT GATE (locked): if over the next 3 batches live (N=1.0+ratchet, the Leash `actual` row) does NOT beat the `atr05` shadow cumulatively вҶ’ revert `atr_mult`вҶ’0.5. Separately, if the ratchet ever clamps a trade that would've re-run вүҘ+0.5% twice вҶ’ raise be_lock toward 0 / review.** D11 wired (panel toggle + lock input + load/save). Sim: the 5 broken trades go from вҲ’0.02/вҲ’1.20 to ~+0.10.
- **рҹҸғ ATR-FLOOR TRAIL (CHANDELIER) вҖ” SHIPPED 2026-06-16 PM (operator, DISCIPLINE-OVERRIDE).** ROOT CAUSE of strpk early-exits: the `KГ—peak_stretch` ratio trail collapses to ~0 width on a freshly-armed (tiny) peak вҶ’ a first bounce trips it before the move develops (AERO closed +0.23% then ran вҲ’6.8%; HYPE +0.30%вҶ’+2.78%; STG +0.50%вҶ’+2.5% вҖ” all post-close, shadow-independent via `post_exit_peak_pnl`). FIX: **ATR-floored give-back** вҖ” exit only when P&L retraces **> NГ—entry_atr_pct** from peak (a normal bounce <1 ATR can't trip it; only a real reversal does). Config `runner_trail_short_use_atr`=true (fallback to ratio when false) + `runner_trail_short_atr_mult`=**N=1.0** (robust default вҖ” would have held all 3 early-exiters; the bounces were 0.04вҖ“0.30 ATR). Live in the realtime flip-strpk block вҶ’ **applies to ALL flip shorts running strpk** (FAN + PAIR_RSI_OB + LONG_UNMATCHED). Hard SL (вҲ’0.70%) still backstops reversers. UI in the рҹҸғ Runner Stretch-Trail (SHORT) panel (D11: toggle + N, load/save). **SHADOW tuning: `shadow_atr05/10/15_pnl` columns** test N=0.5/1.0/1.5 observation-only вҖ” next batch compare them + actual + post_exit_peak to confirm N (0.5 captures more on clean runs but risks mid-trend whipsaw; 1.0 robust; data picks). **REVERT GATE: if actual вҲ’ shadow_tight < 0 cumulative on NвүҘ8 fresh armed shorts вҶ’ strpk/ATR-floor net-harmful, turn OFF (same gate as the strpk promotion).** вҡ пёҸ DISCIPLINE-OVERRIDE: shipped live on N=3 prior FAN flips (pre-Fix-A data) вҖ” validate on the fresh post-deploy batch; if early exits persist under the ATR-floor, the residual is regime (FAN flips in CHOPPY) not the trail.
- **рҹҸғ STRPK MOVED TO REALTIME TICK RESOLUTION (Fix A) вҖ” SHIPPED 2026-06-16 PM (operator).** The flip SHORT runner stretch-trail exit was moved OUT of the 1s monitor (`update_open_positions`) INTO the realtime WS-tick path (`check_realtime_stop_loss`, ~line 8870, right before the tight-trail suppress). - **рҹ”ӯ WATCHLIST (2026-06-17, SHARPENED вҖ” supersedes the liquidityГ—ATR framing) вҖ” flip-SHORT ATRвүҘ2 Г— REGIME, a 2D inversion.** ATR>2 ALONE is non-monotonic noise (pooled >2.00 bucket was 100% WR / +$495 on N=4; high ATR is the *best* bucket). The real axis is **BTC regime, and it runs OPPOSITE to the normal flip-short edge**: across the deduped pool, **ATRвүҘ2 flip-shorts WIN in BULL (3W/0L, +$223, 2 batches) and LOSE in STRONG_BEAR**. MECHANISM: a FAN flip shorts a *parabolic pump*; in a strong bear that pump is a violent **counter-trend short-squeeze** that keeps ripping вҶ’ the short never arms and the high ATR gaps the вҲ’0.70 SL to ~вҲ’1.2 (AGT 2.1, HUSDT 3.0, ESPORTS 4.0 this batch вҖ” all never-armed, all вҲ’1.2). In a bull the same pump is an *exhausting overextension* вҶ’ the fade pays. **вҡ пёҸ INTERACTION: FLIP_SHORT_REGIME has this BACKWARDS for ATRвүҘ2** вҖ” it blocks bull/chopвҲ§ADXО”<0 (which would kill the high-ATR bull *winners*, e.g. HUSDT-W/EVAA-W ADXО”<0) and *exempts* bear (keeping the high-ATR *losers*). **Rule в‘  SHIPPED 2026-06-17 PM (operator-directed) вҖ” cut REFINED вүҘ2 вҶ’ вүҘ3; Rule в‘Ў parked.** в‘  **`flip-SHORT ATRвүҘ3 вҲ§ bear вҶ’ BLOCK` вҖ” LIVE.** `flip_short_atr_block_min=3.0` + `flip_short_atr_block_regimes="STRONG_BEAR,HEALTHY_BEAR,BEAR_EXHAUSTED"`; block in `_flip_filters` gated to `flip_dir=='SHORT'` (reason `FLIP_SHORT_HIATR`, rides `_record_filter_block`); D11 wired (FLIP panel rose row + load/save). **WHY вүҘ3 not вүҘ2:** the cut isn't at 2 вҖ” bear flip-shorts by ATR: 1.5 STG-W/PORTAL-W(+$362), 1.9 EVAA-L, **2.0 BR-W(+$272)**, 2.1 AGT-L, 3.0 HUSDT-L, 4.0 ESPORTS-L. The clean 0%-WR cliff is **ATRвүҘ3 (HUSDT+ESPORTS, вҲ’$245)**; ATR<2.5 bear shorts are net-POSITIVE (PORTAL/BR/STG) so вүҘ2 would kill proven winners. Bull high-ATR shorts WIN (regime inversion) вҶ’ block is bear-only. **DISCIPLINE: N=2/one-window (both ATRвүҘ3 losers from today's bear window) вҖ” operator-directed discipline-override, below bar.** **TIGHT REVERT: re-open (raise min toward 4 or drop the regime) if blocked ATRвүҘ3 bear shorts would have вүҘ40% WR on NвүҘ6 fresh вҖ” track via the phantom/passthrough + the LIVE Flip Trades Г— BTC-Regime table.** Cut may move (вүҘ2.5 vs вүҘ3 vs вүҘ4 unresolved on N=2). в‘Ў **`carve ATRвүҘ2 OUT of FLIP_SHORT_REGIME (bull side) вҶ’ UNBLOCK` вҖ” PARKED (leave blocked).** The filter's вҲ’$691 loser value is **entirely ATR<2** (the ATRвүҘ2 slice of the blocked cell is 2W/0L), so the carve-out would be low-risk вҖ” BUT it's un-earnable by a normal gate: **blocked shorts never fire вҶ’ can't accrue live N вҶ’ "unblock when WRвүҘX on NвүҘY" is a CATCH-22** (operator-caught). Resolutions are only: (a) **leave permanently blocked [CHOSEN default]** вҖ” cohort вүҲ2вҖ“3% of flips, forfeits ~2 frozen-pool winners (HUSDT-W +0.32, EVAA-W +1.65) = negligible, validated filter intact; (b) **unblock-now + a measurable REVERT gate** (re-block if ATRвүҘ2 bullвҲ§ADXО”<0 вүӨ40% WR on NвүҘ6 once firing) вҖ” only if the operator wants the upside, rests on N=2вҖ“3; (c) phantom-instrument the blocked shorts (overkill for 3%). NOT pursuing unless operator opts for (b). The BLOCK candidate в‘  is the live one. - **рҹ”ӯ WATCHLIST (2026-06-17) вҖ” generalize the BE-ratchet to the NORMAL realtime trailing (active, decoupled breakeven floor).** Root cause of VELVET-type round-trips (armed peak +0.76 вҶ’ вҲ’1.20 SL): the realtime trailing pullback trigger is ATR-FLOORED (`_effective_pullback = max(base, entry_atr Г— trailing_atr_multiplier=0.5)`), so on a high-ATR pair (VELVET ATR 1.59%) the give-back needed to ARM the trail is huge вҶ’ it never crosses while in profit (`trailing_first_pullback_pnl_pct = вҲ’1.094` = first crossing was already at вҲ’1.09%) вҶ’ the ATR-widened hard SL is the only exit. **`trailing_min_profit_to_fire`=0.1 does NOT cover this** вҖ” verified at [trading_engine.py:9127](services/trading_engine.py:9127) it's a SUPPRESSOR (cancels an already-triggered trailing close below 0.1, flips-only), the OPPOSITE of a floor вҖ” it removes exits below 0.1, never creates one, and it's COUPLED to the ATR-pullback trigger that didn't fire in time (on VELVET it even suppressed the вҲ’1.09 close вҶ’ SL took it to вҲ’1.20). **PROPOSAL: an active, DECOUPLED BE-ratchet on the realtime path** вҖ” once `running_peak вүҘ be_arm (0.45)`, force a close at `pnl вүӨ be_lock (0.10)` regardless of the ATR-pullback (`reason TRAILING_BE_RATCHET`). Fixed P&L level вҶ’ immune to the high-ATR scaling problem; direction-agnostic (covers flip-longs AND the short side as a backstop). VELVET: would exit ~+0.10 vs вҲ’1.20 (saves ~+1.30); shadow_tight (0.25 P&L give-back) +0.51 confirms a fixed floor works. Config: `trailing_be_ratchet_enabled` + `trailing_be_arm_pct=0.45` + `trailing_be_lock_pct=0.10`. **SCOPE decision pending: flips-only (lower blast radius, where the gap is seen) vs all trailing trades.** Caveat: caps a dip-then-rerun at the lock (bounded вҖ” banks a small win; lower the lock for more room). Note: this is the GENERAL version of the SHORT runner BE-ratchet already shipped (which is ATR-floor-specific + short-only).

- **рҹ”Җвҡ пёҸ FLIP CHAIN-POSITION BUG вҖ” WATCHLIST (identified 2026-06-15, NOT fixed; decision deferred to data).**
  **CORRECT DESIGN (the intent):** the flip should fade ONLY entries that *passed every filter and would have actually traded* but for the fan dead-zone вҖ” i.e. genuine "would-have-opened" longs (fan 0.85-3.00 / 5.0-99) and shorts (fan 1.00-1.90). For that, `FAN_RATIO_GATE` must be the **LAST** gate in the chain, so a fan-blocked entry is guaranteed to have cleared all other filters.
  **ACTUAL DESIGN (what's coded):** `FAN_RATIO_GATE` fires at **gate #8 of ~27** in `scan_and_trade` (line ~6771), and the flip opens *right there* вҖ” BEFORE ~19 downstream gates (`BTC_TREND_FILTER`, `BTC_SLOPE_*`, `BTC_1H_*`, `BTC_ACCEL_CHASE_LONG`, `PAIR_TREND_FILTER`, `VOL_GATE`, `BREADTH_GATE`, PAIR_ATRвҖҰ). So flips fade a **contaminated SUPERSET**: entries that passed only the first 8 filters, NOT all of them. A fan-blocked long that would have failed a downstream gate (e.g. NEAR вҖ” a counter-trend bullish stack in a HEALTHY_BEAR that `BTC_TREND_FILTER`/`PAIR_TREND_FILTER` would likely have killed) still triggers a flip today. (Does NOT change which entries *trade* вҖ” fan-band entries are always blocked either way вҖ” only which ones *flip*; the phantom seeds at the same wrong point, so its +0.13% edge is on the superset too.)
  **COUNTERINTUITIVE TWIST (why not fixed blindly):** the downstream gates block *counter-trend* entries, so the "junk" longs they'd block are exactly the ones whose fade (SHORT) is **macro-aligned** (short with a bear) вҖ” and those won this batch (NEAR +0.40% pk, FARTCOIN +0.63% pk, N=2 = noise). The passed-all-filters longs are in *supportive* regimes вҶ’ their fades are counter-trend-into-the-trend (the cohort steamrolled in STRONG_BULL). So fixing blindly might drop the WINNERS and keep the losers.
  **DECISION GATE (resolve with data, target NвүҘ30 clean flips): deeply evaluate flip WINNERS vs LOSERS вҖ” primarily by REGIME ALIGNMENT (macro-aligned fade vs counter-trend fade, using captured `entry_macro_trend`/`entry_btc_regime`) and the Entry-Conditions-by-Outcome separators.** в‘  If a CLEAR loser-filter emerges (e.g. counter-trend fades lose, aligned win) вҶ’ **KEEP the current mid-chain design and ADD that filter** to remove the losers (a regime-gate, NOT a chain move). в‘Ў If NO clean separator emerges вҶ’ **revert to the CORRECT design: move `FAN_RATIO_GATE` + the flip trigger + the phantom seed to the END of the filter chain** (after `BREADTH_GATE`, before `open_position`), so flips only fire on genuine passed-all-filters entries вҖ” and re-validate the edge on the clean cohort. Until resolved: keep mid-chain (more volume = faster N for the split); cost is low (flip on 1Г— probation, net-negative regardless).
- **рҹ”Җрҹ§Ә REGIME-ALIGNMENT FINDING + FAN_CONTROL / FAN-RATIO-CURVE EXPERIMENT вҖ” shipped 2026-06-15 (phantom/observation-only, forward-only).** **THE FINDING (mechanism-backed, from the 2-batch flip split):** flip winners vs losers separate cleanly on **macro regime alignment, NOT the FAN signal.** A fade that aligns with the BTC EMA20 slope wins (aligned: ~88% WR / +$126 in-sample); a counter-trend fade loses (short into a RISING BTC: ~50% WR / вҲ’$120). Smoking gun = FARTCOIN: same pair, won its fade in a bear window, lost the SAME fade twice in a bull window. **Open question this experiment answers:** is the fan dead-zone (0.85-3.00/5.0-99 long, 1.00-1.90 short) actually *doing* anything, or is it incidental to regime alignment? **Two probes added:** в‘  **FAN_CONTROL phantom** вҖ” a virtual fade seeded when an entry's fan ratio is OUTSIDE the dead-zone (i.e. the entry PASSES the fan filter); it's the A/B control for FAN_RATIO_GATE вҖ” if FAN_CONTROL fades pay the SAME as FAN_RATIO_GATE fades (once regime-matched), the fan band earns nothing and the real signal is pure regime. Seeded in the fan gate's `for-else` branch (loop completes with no band match вҶ’ fan outside dead-zone), fail-silent, never affects live. в‘Ў **FAN-RATIO CURVE** вҖ” a new `рҹ”Җ Phantom Flip` sub-table (`#phantom-fan-curve-body`, both text exports) that pools FAN_RATIO_GATE + FAN_CONTROL phantoms and buckets by fan ratio (0-0.85 / 0.85-1.0 / 1.0-1.35 / 1.35-1.65 / 1.65-2.0 / 2.0-3.0 / 3.0-5.0 / 5.0-99) Г— regime alignment (all / aligned / counter), flagging which buckets are in the dead-zone (DZ). Goal: find WHERE the aligned edge peaks across fan ratio вҶ’ **define the best fan range for fades** (refines or replaces the dead-zone for the flip sleeve). **READ at NвүҘ30 pooled fades/bucket: if the aligned edge is flat across ALL fan buckets (DZ and non-DZ alike) вҶ’ the fan band is incidental; design the live flip sleeve as a pure REGIME-ALIGNMENT gate (fade only when macro-aligned, any fan). If the aligned edge concentrates in specific fan buckets вҶ’ tighten the flip's fan range to those. Either way the live regime-alignment gate (deferred above) gets its fan window from this curve.** Friction wall still applies: phantom is frictionless, live pays ~0.27%/trade вҶ’ +0.30% promotion bar on any bucket before it ships live.

## Metrics tracked
**Avg P&L %** (leverage-invariant вҖ” the comparison metric) В· Daily Compound Return В· per-cell verdict (Multiplier / Pattern-Cell Ship tables) В· Filter Blocks counters В· Gross gauge (% + $ tooltip) В· entry/exit slippage В· Pattern C/W trackers (observation-only).

## Known risks
- **Gross 30Г— tail**: a вҲ’3.3% correlated gap вүҲ вҲ’100% equity (per-position SLs are primary protection; gross cap is flash-crash insurance).
- **Multiplier amplification on fat-tail losers**: C6/C1/W2 cohorts are 62-74% WR *winners* net-dragged by a few 3Г—-amplified losers вҶ’ fix is surgical sizing on the specific losers, NOT blocking the cohort ("high-WR-but-net-losing" trap).
- **LONG book structurally weak** (negative in most cross-batch dimensions); LONG vol floor occasionally clips high-ATR runners.

## Do not change for now
- **BE stays OFF** (proven not to help; runner-trail + trailing is the current exit thesis (FAST_EXIT OFF too)).
- **SHORT volume rescue stays $0** (mirroring LONG $50M would un-block dead-tape SHORTs like SEI).
- **Don't add more entry filters reflexively** вҖ” 15+ already, diminishing returns. Exit-side + sizing is the active lever.

## Next ~1-week forward-test focus
1. **Liquidity-sizing live validation** вҖ” the Go-Live Watch signals (Gross gauge, GROSS_CAP_SKIP, в‘  slippage, REDEPLOY_OPEN=0).
2. **Global Vol filter** firing correctly + not clipping runners (VOL_GATE counters).
3. **ADX О” filter** + the recent BTC RSI/ADX cross-filter openings holding.
4. Combined **Avg P&L %** vs the recent вҲ’$1,941/207-trade baseline; SHORT-side drag (dead-tape, C1/W2 amplified losers).
5. **Reset partition:** after the user's reset, analyze only `opened_at вүҘ reset timestamp` (don't pool pre-reset trades).
